xml:space="preserve" bytes="419944"> {{Article for deletion/dated|page=List of mosques in the United States|timestamp=20140719100923|year=2014|month=July|day=19|substed=yes|help=off}} {{dablinks|date=July 2014}} The overall number of mosques in the United States quietly rose from 1,209 in 2000 to 2,106 in 2010. The number of Islamic places of worship in the United States soared 74% in the past decade.http://usatoday30.usatoday.com/news/religion/story/2012-02-29/islamic-worship-growth-us/53298792/1 The study — The American Mosque 2011 — was sponsored by the [[Hartford Institute for Religion Research]] (Hartford Seminary), the [[Association of Statisticians of American Religious Bodies]], as well as the nation's largest Islamic civic and religious groups, including the [[Islamic Society of North America]] and the [[Council on American-Islamic Relations]]. The study finds that states with the most mosques are New York (257), California (246) and Texas (166).http://usatoday30.usatoday.com/news/religion/story/2012-02-29/islamic-worship-growth-us/53298792/1 This is a '''list of [[mosque]]s in the United States of America''' in alphabetical order by
